SELECT [p1].[SalesOrderId], COUNT(DISTINCT ([p1].[PaymentId])) AS [Count]
FROM [Payments] AS [p]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [p0].[PaymentId], [p0].[SalesOrderId]
    FROM [PaymentAllocations] AS [p0]
    WHERE [p0].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit)
) AS [p1] ON [p].[Id] = [p1].[PaymentId]
WHERE [p].[IsDeleted] = CAST(0 AS bit) AND [p].[TenantId] = @__tenantId_0 AND [p].[CreatedAt] >= @__from_1 AND [p].[Status] = 3
GROUP BY [p1].[SalesOrderId]
HAVING COUNT(DISTINCT ([p1].[PaymentId])) > 1
